Section 10.01\tab Disposition of Tangible Personal Property by Memorandum
\par }\pard \ltrpar\qj \li720\ri0\sa200\sl276\slmult1\widctlpar\wrapdefault\aspalpha\aspnum\faauto\adjustright\rin0\lin720\itap0\pararsid10426501 {\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 (a)}{
\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \tab \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 Grantor may identify for in-kind distribution\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
 to any person, including to any beneficiary who would otherwise receive a residuary share of trust property under this Trust Agreement, a specific item, or specific items, of tangible personal property by a signed, written memorandum executed after the G
\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 r\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
antor signs this Trust Agreement.  The memorandum must refer to the Trust and must reasonably identify the items and the person designated to receive each item.  If the Grantor executes a memorandum, the Trustee shall incorporate the memorandum by referen
\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 c\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 e into this Trust Agreement to the extent permitted by law.
\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 (b)}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \tab \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
The Trustee shall distribute the items of tangible personal property listed in the memorandum as promptly as practicable after the death of the Grantor, together with any insurance policies co\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
vering the property and any claims under those policies, as provided in the memorandum.  If the Grantor leaves multiple written memoranda that conflict as to the disposition of any item of tangible personal property, the memorandum with the most recent da
\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 t\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 e will control as to that item.
\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 (c)}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \tab \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
If the law does not permit incorporation of the memorandum by reference, the memorandum will then serve as an amendment to the Trust, but only to the extent the amendment disposes of tangible personal property.  The Grantor requests that the Trustee follo
\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 w\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0  Grantor\hich\f0 \rquote \loch\f0 s wishes and distribute in-kind the items of tangible personal property listed in a memorandum according to its terms.
\par }\pard \ltrpar\qj \li0\ri0\sa200\sl276\slmult1\widctlpar\wrapdefault\aspalpha\aspnum\faauto\adjustright\rin0\lin0\itap0\pararsid10426501 {\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
Section 10.02\tab Administration and Priority of In-Kind Distributions Designated by Grantor

\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \tab \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 All in-kind distributions by memora\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
ndum shall have priority over and shall be calculated, set aside, and allocated to the designated beneficiary by the Trustee prior to the distribution of trust property to Grantor\hich\f0 \rquote \loch\f0 
s residuary beneficiaries referenced in Section 6.02.
\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 (b)}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \tab \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 If a designated in

\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 h\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 all diminish the Trustee\hich\f0 \rquote \loch\f0 s authority to make any gift or distribution in kind to any person or beneficiary within the Trustee\hich\f0 \rquote \loch\f0 
s discretion, as authorized elsewhere in this Trust Agreement.
\par }\pard \ltrpar\qj \li720\ri0\sa200\sl276\slmult1\widctlpar\wrapdefault\aspalpha\aspnum\faauto\adjustright\rin0\lin720\itap0\pararsid1249054 {\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 (c)}{

Section 11.01\tab Maximum Term of Tr\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 ust
\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
Notwithstanding any other provision of this Trust Agreement to the contrary, unless terminated earlier under other provisions of the Trust, any non-vested property interest or power of appointment created under the Trust will terminate no later than 21
\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
 years after the last to die of the beneficiaries who are living as of the execution of this Trust Agreement, or no later than the maximum term permitted by <4> law, whichever is greater. At that time, the remaining trust property will vest in and be dist
\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 r\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 ibuted to the beneficiaries pursuant to Article Six.
\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 Section 11.02\tab Spendthrift Provision
\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
No beneficiary of any trust created under this Trust Agreement may assign, anticipate, encumber, alienate, or otherwise voluntarily transfer the income or principal of any trust created under this Trust.  In addition, neither the income nor the principal 
\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 o\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
f any trust created under this Trust Agreement is subject to attachment, bankruptcy proceedings or any other legal process, the interference or control of creditors or others, or any involuntary transfer.  This Section does not restrict a beneficiary
\hich\f0 \rquote \loch\f0 s ri\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 g\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 ht to disclaim any interest or exercise of any power of appointment granted in this Trust Agreement.
\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 Section 11.03\tab Contest Provision
\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 If any person directly or indirectly attempts to contest or oppose the validity of the Trust, or commences, continues, or p
\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
rosecutes any legal proceedings to set the Trust aside, then that person will forfeit his or her share, cease to have any right or interest in the trust property, and will, for purposes of the Trust, be deemed to have predeceased the death of the Grantor.

\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 Section 11.04\tab Survivorship Presumption

If any beneficiary under this Trust is living at the death of the Grantor, but dies within 30 days after the death of the Grantor, then the beneficiary will be considered to have predeceased the Grantor.

\par }\pard \ltrpar\qj \li720\ri0\sa200\sl276\slmult1\widctlpar\wrapdefault\aspalpha\aspnum\faauto\adjustright\rin0\lin720\itap0\pararsid11878109 {\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 (a)
\tab Multiple Originals; Validity of Paper or Electronic Copies}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 .\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0  \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
This Trust may be executed in any number of counterparts, each of \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
which will be considered an original. Any person may rely on a paper or electronic copy of this Trust that the Trustee certifies to be a true copy as if it were an original.
\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid11878109 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 (b)\tab Singular and Plural; Gender}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 .\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0

ords may be construed as plural, and plural words may be construed as singular.  Words of one gender may be construed as denoting another gender as is appropriate within the context.  The word \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 or,
\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0  when used in a list of more than two items, may function as\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0  both a conjunction and a disjunction as the context requires.
\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid11878109 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 (c)\tab Headings of Articles, Sections, and Subsections}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 .

\par \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 (}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid11878109 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 d)\tab Governing State Law}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501

d, construed, and administered according to the laws of the state of <4>, as amended, except as to Trust property required by law to be governed by the laws of another jurisdiction and unless the situs of administration is changed pursuant to <4> law.

\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid11878109 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 (e)\tab \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 Notices}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 
\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
. Unless otherwise stated, any notice required under this Trust will be in writing.  The notice may be personally delivered with proof of delivery to the party requiring notice and will be effective on the date personally delivered.  Notice may also
\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
 be mailed, postage prepaid, by certified mail with return receipt requested to the last known address of the party requiring notice.  Mailed notice is effective on the date of the return receipt.  If a party giving notice does not receive the return rece
\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 i\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
pt but has proof that he or she mailed the notice, notice will be effective on the date it would normally have been received via certified mail.  If the party requiring notice is a minor or incapacitated individual, notice will be given to the parent or l
\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 e\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 gal representative.
\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid11878109 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 (f)\tab Severability}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0\afs24 \ltrch\fcs0 \f0\fs24\insrsid726253\charrsid10426501 \hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
. The invalidity or unenforceability of any provision of this Trust does not affect the validity or enforceability of any other provision of this Trust.  If a court of competent jurisdiction determines that any provision\hich\af0\dbch\af31505\loch\f0 
 is invalid, the remaining provisions of this Trust are to be interpreted as if the invalid provision had never been included.
